<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-format">Featured</span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>

</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>To the North of the city of SAA has broken the resistance of the militants in Ayyash district, and is developing a successful offensive along the road leading to Madan, which is cut off from the main territory of the Caliphate.</p>

<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/22/exclusive-turkey-to-deploy-troops-inside-syrias-idlib-erdogan-reuters/" rel="bookmark" title="00:30"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-22T00:30:00+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-22</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>

</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>Turkish President Tayyip Erdogan said on Thursday Turkey will deploy troops in Syria’s northern Idlib region as part of a so-called de-escalation agreement brokered by Russia last month.</p>
</div><!-- .entry-summary -->

<h1 class="entry-title"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/22/breaking-isis-agrees-to-surrender-hama-amn/" rel="bookmark">ISIS agrees to surrender Hama | AMN</a></h1>
<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/22/breaking-isis-agrees-to-surrender-hama-amn/" rel="bookmark" title="00:27"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-22T00:27:30+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-22</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>
<span class="comments-link"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/22/breaking-isis-agrees-to-surrender-hama-amn/#respond">Leave a comment</a></span>
</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>According to Al-Masdar News correspondent Ibrahim Joudeh, jihadist militants have already begun to leave the villages and towns of Soha, Abu Hubailat, Akash, Al-Barghouthyah and Umm Mil, all located along the M-45 highway in the southeastern countryside of Hama.</p>

<h1 class="entry-title"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/22/the-attack-of-al-nusra-in-northern-hama-colonel-cassad/" rel="bookmark">The attack of “al-Nusra” in Northern Hama | Colonel Cassad</a></h1>
<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/22/the-attack-of-al-nusra-in-northern-hama-colonel-cassad/" rel="bookmark" title="00:13"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-22T00:13:36+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-22</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>
<span class="comments-link"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/22/the-attack-of-al-nusra-in-northern-hama-colonel-cassad/#respond">Leave a comment</a></span>
</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>Judging by the nature of the events, the preparation of the insurgents’ attack was revealed in advance, which led to effective countermeasures, which led to the failure of the offensive in such a short time. A striking contrast with the March events in Northern Hama. By the evening of September 20, according to Syrian sources, the militants were driven out of those areas that they managed to occupy at the cost of large losses, and now the issue of the counteroffensive of the SAA towards Murak is on the agenda in order to take advantage of the consequences of the unsuccessful offensive by militants.</p>

<h1 class="entry-title"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/trump-goes-full-bushtard-at-the-un/" rel="bookmark">Trump goes full Bushtard at the UN</a></h1>
<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/trump-goes-full-bushtard-at-the-un/" rel="bookmark" title="01:58"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-20T01:58:15+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-20</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>

<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>Despite some of his “America First” rhetoric – tossed in as red meat to his “base” – Trump revealed a global outlook that differed from the Bush-Obama neoconservative/liberal-interventionist approach in words only. In substance, Trump appears to be just the latest American poodle on Bibi Netanyahu’s leash.</p>

<header class="entry-header">
<h1 class="entry-title"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/alexander-dugin-settlement-of-the-karabakh-conflict-unprofitable-for-the-globalist-elite/" rel="bookmark">Alexander Dugin: Settlement of the Karabakh conflict unprofitable for the globalist elite</a></h1>
<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/alexander-dugin-settlement-of-the-karabakh-conflict-unprofitable-for-the-globalist-elite/" rel="bookmark" title="01:52"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-20T01:52:29+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-20</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>
<span class="comments-link"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/alexander-dugin-settlement-of-the-karabakh-conflict-unprofitable-for-the-globalist-elite/#respond">Leave a comment</a></span>
</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>In my opinion, the decision on the five regions gives us a partial solution to the Nagorno-Karabakh conflict. And the resolution of the Karabakh problem strengthens the positions of states, and not only Azerbaijan, Armenia and Russia, but also Turkey, creates a system for a balanced and balanced model of geopolitical stability and security in the South Caucasus, and accordingly, freedom of action for “chaos sellers” is reduced. That is, in fact, the model of geopolitical coexistence between Russia, Azerbaijan, Turkey, Armenia and Iran is disadvantageous only to those who are not on this list. We, as neighbors, can not get anywhere from each other. And we will always live in the same space</p>
</div><!-- .entry-summary -->

<header class="entry-header">
<h1 class="entry-title"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/alexander-dugin-aliyev-made-azerbaijan-sovereign/" rel="bookmark">Alexander Dugin: Aliyev made Azerbaijan sovereign</a></h1>
<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/alexander-dugin-aliyev-made-azerbaijan-sovereign/" rel="bookmark" title="01:37"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-20T01:37:40+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-20</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>
<span class="comments-link"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/alexander-dugin-aliyev-made-azerbaijan-sovereign/#respond">Leave a comment</a></span>
</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>Azerbaijan during the reign of Ilham Aliyev became a full-fledged, strong, wealthy and established sovereign state. This is a rare case among the states of the post-Soviet space, since not all have managed to cope with the fact that they truly ensure the sovereignty and development of their own country.</p>
</div><!-- .entry-summary -->

<h1 class="entry-title"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/turkish-troops-on-the-border-with-kurdistan-colonel-cassad/" rel="bookmark">Turkish troops on the border with Kurdistan | Colonel Cassad</a></h1>
<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/turkish-troops-on-the-border-with-kurdistan-colonel-cassad/" rel="bookmark" title="01:18"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-20T01:18:51+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-20</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>
<span class="comments-link"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/turkish-troops-on-the-border-with-kurdistan-colonel-cassad/#respond">Leave a comment</a></span>
</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>Taking into account possible escalation in Iraq at the end of September, this military activity looks like a pre-preperation “just in case”, though perhaps the Turkish General staff has a more serious agreement with the Iranian military on the subject of action to prevent the dismemberment of Iraq. The official explanation from the Turkish military emphasized that the military exercises are aimed at practicing cooperation in fighting terrorism. As DAESH is long gone from the area, it is quite clear who the Turks mean.</p>
</div><!-- .entry-summary -->

<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/turkey-completes-the-concentration-of-troops-on-the-border-with-idlib-colonel-cassad/" rel="bookmark" title="00:58"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-20T00:58:25+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-20</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>
<span class="comments-link"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/turkey-completes-the-concentration-of-troops-on-the-border-with-idlib-colonel-cassad/#respond">Leave a comment</a></span>
</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>Work continues on the transfer of Turkish armored vehicles to the Turkish-Syrian border, where Turkey shares a border with Idlib.</p>
<p>Apparently they are really preparing the deployment of Turkish troops in the Western districts of Idlib to take control of the border and remove “Al-Nusra”.</p>
</div><!-- .entry-summary -->

<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/the-russian-defense-ministry-has-responded-to-claims-by-the-united-states-colonel-cassad/" rel="bookmark" title="00:52"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-20T00:52:22+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-20</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>

</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>Russian combat aircraft in Syria launched surgical strikes, the U.S. was informed in advance about the limits of military operations in the city of Deir ez-Zor, said on Sunday the official representative of the defense Ministry major-General Igor Konashenkov.</p>

<h1 class="entry-title"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/race-for-syrian-oil-colonel-cassad/" rel="bookmark">Race for Syrian oil | Colonel Cassad</a></h1>
<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/race-for-syrian-oil-colonel-cassad/" rel="bookmark" title="00:48"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-20T00:48:09+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-20</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>
<span class="comments-link"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/race-for-syrian-oil-colonel-cassad/#respond">Leave a comment</a></span>
</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>A visual map illustrating one of the reasons for the race in the province of Deir ez-Zor. Major deposits of oil are still on the territory controlled by the Caliphate and it is the desire to control it that is behind the increased competition between the SAA and the SDF, although of course this problem is not exhausted.</p>
</div><!-- .entry-summary -->

<h1 class="entry-title"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/the-crossing-colonel-cassad/" rel="bookmark">The Crossing | Colonel Cassad</a></h1>
<div class="entry-meta">
<span class="entry-date"><a href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/2017/09/20/the-crossing-colonel-cassad/" rel="bookmark" title="00:43"><time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-09-20T00:43:02+00:00" pubdate="">2017-09-20</time></a></span><span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://4threvolutionarywar.wordpress.com/author/karlvavilov/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Akira">Akira</a></span></span>

</header><!-- .entry-header -->
<div class="entry-summary clear-fix">
<p>The Russian foreign Ministry said that the SAA was able to cross the Euphrates near Deir ez-Zor, the true place of crossing was not specified. Also, it is claimed that the Northern Bank of the Euphrates created a springboard.</p>

<script type="text/javascript">
			( function () {

				var setupPrivacy = function() {

					// Minimal Mozilla Cookie library
					// https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Document/cookie/Simple_document.cookie_framework
					var cookieLib = window.cookieLib = {getItem:function(e){return e&&decodeURIComponent(document.cookie.replace(new RegExp("(?:(?:^|.*;)\\s*"+encodeURIComponent(e).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g,"\\$&")+"\\s*\\=\\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$"),"$1"))||null},setItem:function(e,o,n,t,r,i){if(!e||/^(?:expires|max\-age|path|domain|secure)$/i.test(e))return!1;var c="";if(n)switch(n.constructor){case Number:c=n===1/0?"; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT":"; max-age="+n;break;case String:c="; expires="+n;break;case Date:c="; expires="+n.toUTCString()}return"rootDomain"!==r&&".rootDomain"!==r||(r=(".rootDomain"===r?".":"")+document.location.hostname.split(".").slice(-2).join(".")),document.cookie=encodeURIComponent(e)+"="+encodeURIComponent(o)+c+(r?"; domain="+r:"")+(t?"; path="+t:"")+(i?"; secure":""),!0}};

					// Implement IAB USP API.
					window.__uspapi = function( command, version, callback ) {

						if ( typeof callback !== 'function' ) {
							return;
						}

						if ( command !== 'getUSPData' || version !== 1 ) {
							callback( null, false );
							return;
						}

						// Check for GPC.
						if ( navigator.globalPrivacyControl ) {
							callback( { version: 1, uspString: '1YYN' }, true );
							return;
						}

						// Check for cookie.
						var consent = cookieLib.getItem( 'usprivacy' );

						if ( null === consent ) {
							callback( null, false );
							return;
						}

						callback( { version: 1, uspString: consent }, true );
					};

					// Initialization.
					document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', function() {

						var setDefaultOptInCookie = function() {
							var value = '1YNN';
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'usprivacy', value, 365 * 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						};

						var setCcpaAppliesCookie = function( value ) {
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'ccpa_applies', value, 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						}

						var maybeCallDoNotSellCallback = function() {
							if ( 'function' === typeof window.doNotSellCallback ) {
								return window.doNotSellCallback();
							}

							return false;
						}

						var usprivacyCookie = cookieLib.getItem( 'usprivacy' );

						if ( null !== usprivacyCookie ) {
							maybeCallDoNotSellCallback();
							return;
						}

						var ccpaCookie = cookieLib.getItem( 'ccpa_applies' );

						if ( null === ccpaCookie ) {

							var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
							request.open( 'GET', 'https://public-api.wordpress.com/geo/', true );

							request.onreadystatechange = function () {
								if ( 4 === this.readyState ) {
									if ( 200 === this.status ) {

										var data = JSON.parse( this.response );
										var ccpa_applies = data['region'] && data['region'].toLowerCase() === 'california';

										setCcpaAppliesCookie( ccpa_applies );

										if ( ccpa_applies ) {
											if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
												setDefaultOptInCookie();
											}
										}
									} else {
										setCcpaAppliesCookie( true );
										if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
											setDefaultOptInCookie();
										}
									}
								}
							};

							request.send();
						} else {
							if ( ccpaCookie === 'true' ) {
								if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
									setDefaultOptInCookie();
								}
							}
						}
					} );
				};

				if ( window.defQueue && defQueue.isLOHP && defQueue.isLOHP === 2020 ) {
					defQueue.items.push( setupPrivacy );
				} else {
					setupPrivacy();
				}

			} )();
		</script>

<script>
		// Initialize and attach hovercards to all gravatars
		( function() {
			function init() {
				if ( typeof Gravatar === 'undefined' ) {
					return;
				}

				if ( typeof Gravatar.init !== 'function' ) {
					return;
				}

				Gravatar.profile_cb = function ( hash, id ) {
					WPGroHo.syncProfileData( hash, id );
				};

				Gravatar.my_hash = WPGroHo.my_hash;
				Gravatar.init( 'body', '#wp-admin-bar-my-account' );
			}

			if ( document.readyState !== 'loading' ) {
				init();
			} else {
				document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', init );
			}
		} )();
	</script>
